! Title: AdBlock Filter Lite
! Description: 适用于 AdGuard 的去广告合并规则，每 8 个小时更新一次。规则源：EasyList Optimized、EasyList China Optimized、AdGuard Mobile Ads Optimized、CJX's Annoyance List、Crystal RainSlide CN、Crystal RainSlide Intl、AWAvenue Ads Rule、Xinggsf Rule、NoAppDownload。Lite 版仅针对国内域名拦截。
